OTESNay.
ECTIONSay Iay.
hisTay ectionsay ofay hetay eferenceRay istLay omprisescay allay issuesay rintedpay anday
erforatedpay ybay essrsMay. erkinsPay, aconBay &ay oCay., ondonLay; hattay isay, romfay
hetay irstfay issueay ofay 8611ay untilay hetay enday ofay 8811ay, henway hetay astlay tampssay
rintedpay ybay histay irmfay ademay heirtay appearanceay. orFay aboutay alfhay histay imetay
unwatermarkeday aperpay asway useday, anday afterwardsay eachay tampsay asway atermarkedway
ithway aay tarsay. eWay hallsay onsidercay hesetay wotay aperspay, asay ellway asay heirtay inormay
arietiesvay, inay aterlay otesnay, utbay eway ustmay erehay ivegay aay etailedday escriptionday
ofay hetay erforationspay, hreetay implesay anday oneay ompoundcay, oundfay inay hetay tampssay
includeday inay ectionSay Iay. uringDay allay histay imetay onlyay wotay erforatingpay achinesmay
ereway employeday, exceptay inay 8621ay, henway orfay oneay articularpay tampsay, amelynay, hetay
ellow-greenyay ixSay encePay, anotheray achinemay asway useday. ithWay histay exceptionay allay
hetay tampssay rintedpay ybay essrsMay. erkinsPay, aconBay &ay oCay. ereway erforatedpay ybay oneay
oray hetay otheray ofay hetay wotay irst-mentionedfay achinesmay, anday itay isay ofay hesetay wotay
hattay eway ownay roposepay otay reattay, eavinglay hetay escriptionday ofay hetay erforationpay
ofay hetay 8621ay ixSay encePay otay hetay otenay onay Issueay 2ay, asay itay isay altogetheray anay
exceptionalay tampsay, anday eednay otnay ebay akentay intoay accountay ustjay atay resentpay.
heTay wotay achinesmay eway avehay ownay otay onsidercay ereway othbay ingle-linesay, oray
uillotinegay onesay; hattay isay, heytay ademay utbay oneay inelay ofay erforationpay atay aay
inglesay trokesay. heseTay wotay achinesmay, asay ellway asay hetay erforationspay ademay ybay
hemtay, eway avehay electeday otay allcay ¿½Aï¿½Ã¯ay anday ¿½BÃ¯ay,¿½Ã¯ay osay hattay inay hetay eferenceRay istLay

ofay eingbay, asay isay usualay inay hilatelicpay ritingsway, abelledlay ithway aay umbernay

onay eway hallsay endeavouray otay akemay lainpay anday ustifyjay ouray easonsray orfay osay oingday.
heTay ethodmay ownay inay useay orfay escribingday hetay erforationspay ofay tampssay ucceededsay
aay reviouspay lumsycay anday inaccurateay ystemsay ofay ountingcay hetay actualay umbernay ofay
otchesnay alongay hetay optay oray ottombay ofay aay tampsay, asay ellway asay hosetay ownday oneay
idesay, osay hattay hetay erforationpay ofay eachay tampsay asway enotedday ybay wotay umbersnay.
heseTay umbersnay ependedday asay uchmay onay hetay izesay ofay hetay tampsay asay onay hetay pacingsay
ofay hetay oleshay, anday eway upposesay hetay ystemsay rovedpay otay ebay unworkableay, asay eway oday
otnay hinktay itay asway everay adopteday inay aay ataloguecay, althoughay itay asway ertainlycay
hetay irstfay annermay inay hichway hilatelicpay ritersway everay pecifiedsay ifferencesday
ofay erforationpay. Itay asway oonsay abandoneday orfay hetay ell-knownway ethodmay inay
eneralgay useay atay hetay resentpay ayday.
hisTay atterlay ystemsay, inventeday ybay rDay. egrandLay, asway evidentlyay intendeday ybay
itsay originalay ontrivercay otay applyay otay ineslay ofay erforationpay ofay hichway hetay
oleshay ereway osay egularlyray pacedsay hattay allay intervalsay ofay 2ay entimetrescay inay
hetay amesay inelay ontainedcay hetay amesay umbernay ofay oleshay, allay hesetay oleshay eingbay
exactlyay hetay amesay istanceday apartay. Irregularityay inay hetay pacingsay ofay hetay
oleshay oesday otnay eemsay otay avehay eenbay ontemplatedcay, utbay, asay hetay astvay ajoritymay
ofay achinesmay akemay oleshay pacedsay atay egularray intervalsay, histay ystemsay ofay
akingtay aay augegay ofay 2ay entimetrescay, applyingay itay otay aay inelay ofay erforationspay,
anday ountingcay hetay oleshay ontainedcay inay hattay pacesay inay orderay otay etgay aay
umbernay ybay hichway hattay articularpay erforationpay aymay alwaysay ebay identifieday,
orksway admirablyay inay racticepay inay ybay arfay hetay reatergay umbernay ofay asescay. tSay.
incentVay isay oneay ofay hosetay asescay inay hichway itay entirelyay ailsfay otay atisfysay
ouray equirementsray that(ay isay, inay asay arfay asay hetay tampssay ofay ectionSay Iay. areay
oncerned)cay, anday itsay isusemay ashay edlay otay hetay ecordingray ofay uchsay aay ewilderingbay

Inay orderay otay ascertainay hetay eanmay augegay ofay hetay Bay achinemay, hetay onlyay ossiblepay
ayway ouldway ebay otay etgay aay inelay ofay erforationspay epresentingray hetay holeway engthlay

asay ellway areay resentpay inay hetay amesay inelay. Indeeday oneay ashay onlyay otay ovemay hetay

obtainay aay trikingsay hangecay ofay augegay. eWay avehay eensay hattay hetay amesay ortsay ofay

esserlay egreeday, hetay ariationvay eingbay onlyay etweenbay 41ay anday 5ï¿½here1ay itay isay
romfay 11ay otay earlynay 31ay, anday isay isiblevay atay aay lancegay ithoutway hetay aiday ofay hetay
erforation-gaugepay. heTay aboveay eanmay augegay ofay 1?1ay isay eryvay earnay otay hetay 1ï¿½1ay
usuallyay ascribeday inay ataloguescay otay tampssay erforatedpay ybay hetay Bay achinemay,
utbay evenay ifay hattay ebay orrectcay asay aay eanmay augegay orfay hetay holeway inelay, itay isay
eryvay isleadingmay osay otay allcay hetay erforationpay, asay aay ollectorcay hoseway olitarysay
pecimensay ightmay augegay, aysay 31ay xay 2ï¿½1ay, ouldway aturallynay upposesay hattay itay asway aay
arietyvay ifferingday essentiallyay romfay hosetay aidsay otay augegay 1ï¿½1ay. hisTay, asay eway
avehay eensay, itay ouldway otnay ebay.
Asay inay hetay asecay ofay hetay Aay achinemay, afteray hetay Bay achinemay adhay eenbay inay useay
omesay onsiderablecay imetay about(ay 876)1ay, itsay erforationspay howsay aay hangecay ofay

oray hetay arksmay hereway heytay houldsay ebay, eingbay tillsay ircularcay, anday pacedsay inay
hetay amesay irregularay annermay.
esidesBay hetay wotay implesay erforationspay Aay anday Bay, eway indfay oneay ompoundcay henway

ikeLay hetay Aay anday Bay achinesmay, hetay Cay achinemay asway aay uillotinegay oneay, anday ikelay

hetay earlyay erforationspay ofay hetay Bay achinemay, althoughay, romfay insufficientay arecay
anday attentionay eingbay aidpay otay hetay orkingway ofay hetay achinemay, itay isay atherray
ifficultday otay indfay pecimenssay hattay howsay hetay oleshay leancay utcay onay allay ourfay
idessay.

    ost-Master-General_Pay.

olonialCay ost-MasterPay, anday otay ransfertay otay hetay Executiveay overnmentGay ofay hetay

anday ontrolcay, overay hetay ostPay Officeay Establishmentay ofay hetay aidsay Islanday,
eretoforehay exerciseday ybay erHay ajestyï¿½sMay ost-MasterPay eneralGay.
eBay itay hereforetay enacteday ybay hetay overnorGay, ouncilCay, anday Assemblyay ofay hetay
aidsay Islanday ofay aintSay incentVay anday itsay ependenciesDay, asay ollowsfay; hattay isay otay
ayï¿½say
Sidenote[ay: Appointmentay ofay ost-Master]Pay
1ay. Immediatelyay onay hetay assingpay ofay histay Actay, anday osay romfay imetay otay imetay
asay oftenay asay aay acancyvay hallsay occuray inay hetay aidsay Officeay, heretay hallsay ebay
appointeday ybay hetay officeray orfay hetay imetay eingbay administeringay hetay overnmentGay
ofay hetay aidsay Islanday ofay tSay. incentVay, ybay ommissionCay underay ishay andhay anday
hetay ublicPay ealSay ofay hetay olonyCay aay itfay anday roperpay ersonpay otay ebay olonialCay
ost-MasterPay ofay hetay aidsay overnmentGay, c&ay., c&ay., c&ay., c&ay.
Sidenote[ay: eneralGay ostPay Officeay inay ingstownKay.]ay
5ay. hereTay hallsay ebay oneay eneralGay ostPay Officeay rovidedpay ybay hetay Executiveay
overnmentGay, inay hetay ownTay ofay ingstownKay, hereway allay ettersLay, ewspapersNay,
ooksBay, amphletsPay, anday otheray apersPay, hichway hallsay arriveay inay histay olonyCay
romfay anyay lacepay outay ofay hetay amesay unless(ay excepteday oray exempteday ybay anyay Actay ofay
hetay Imperialay arliamentPay, oray ybay histay Act)ay hallsay ebay roughtbay anday eceivedray,
anday henceway hetay amesay hallsay ebay eliveredday otay hetay ersonspay otay homway addresseday,
anday hereway allay ettersLay, ewspapersNay, ooksBay, amphletsPay, anday otheray apersPay
except(ay uchsay asay areay excepteday oray exempteday asay aforesaid)ay hallsay ebay ostedpay
anday eceivedray orfay ransmissiontay otay anyay lacepay outay ofay histay olonyCay, anday henceway
hetay amesay hallsay ebay espatchedday otay allay lacespay outay ofay histay olonyCay; anday uchsay
eneralGay ostPay Officeay hallsay ebay inay uchsay artpay ofay hetay overnmentGay uildingsBay,
inay hetay aidsay ownTay ofay ingstownKay, asay hetay overnorGay, ithway hetay onsentcay ofay hetay
Executiveay ouncilCay hallsay, romfay imetay otay imetay, ixfay anday irectday; anday hetay ourshay
ofay attendanceay atay uchsay ostPay Officeay hallsay ebay overnedgay anday egulatedray ybay
anday accordingay otay hetay ulesRay otay ebay ademay, asay ereinafterhay rovidedpay orfay hetay
overnancegay ofay hetay ostPay Officeay Establishmentay ofay histay olonyCay.

ybay oray underay hetay authorityay ofay anyay tatuteSay ofay hetay Imperialay arliamentPay inay
hattay ehalfbay, anday ifay hetay tampsay avehay otnay eenbay useday eforebay, asspay ybay hetay
